Antarctica_GUI_setup = {

	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Scope_Array 					# holds the scope for each tile
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Numbers_Array 					# holds the number for each tile
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array			# holds the mission progress for each tile
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array 	# holds the mission source scope (who started the mission) for each tile
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array 	# holds the mission target scope (whose territory the mission was started in) for each tile
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Id_Array 				# holds the mission number for each tile
	
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Tile	 				# holds the list of tile locations of all completed missions
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Dates 				# holds the list of dates of all completed missions
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Source	 			# holds the list of source tags of all completed missions
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Target	 			# holds the list of target tags of all completed missions
	clear_array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_IDs	 				# holds the list of IDs of all completed missions
	
	setup_Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Scope_Array_initial = yes
	set_variable = { global.AA_Num = 1 }
	
	for_each_loop = {
		array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Scope_Array
		value = v
		index = i
		
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Numbers_Array
			value = global.AA_Num
		}
		
		add_to_variable = { global.AA_Num = 1 }
		
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array
			value = 0
		}
		
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array
			value = 0
		}
		
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array
			value = 0
		}
		
		add_to_array = {
			array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Id_Array
			value = 0
		}
	}

	USA = {
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending_Display = 60 }
		set_variable = { econ_Antarctica_GUI_Foreign_Budget_slider_pct = 60 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending = 0.06 }
		multiply_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending = 26 } # Yearly
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Supply_to_be_Sent = Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending_Display }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = Antarctica_Agency_Supply_to_be_Sent
			max = 100
		}
		round_variable = Antarctica_Agency_Supply_to_be_Sent
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Decay_Reduction = Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending_Display }
		subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Decay_Reduction = 50 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = Antarctica_Agency_Decay_Reduction
			max = 50
		}
		round_variable = Antarctica_Agency_Decay_Reduction
		multiply_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Decay_Reduction = 0.01 }
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending_Frequency = 3 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Supply_Shipment_Time = 14 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending_BiMonthly = 1 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending_Monthly = 1 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending_BiWeekly = 2 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Agency_Budget_Spending_Weekly = 1 }
		
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 0
			end = 61
			value = i

			add_to_array = { Antarctica_GUI_Foreign_Budget_set_buttons_array = i }
		}
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Foreign_Budget_slider_dot_x = econ_Antarctica_GUI_Foreign_Budget_slider_pct }
		multiply_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Foreign_Budget_slider_dot_x = 1.88 }

		limit = { is_Antarctic_nation = yes }
		set_country_flag = country_has_gui # for the bottom gui tab
		set_country_flag = TNO_econ_help_arrows_dismissed

		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Selected_State = -1 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Selected_Scope = -1 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Scope = THIS }
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Main_Zoom_Array^0 = 0 }

		set_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = Antarctica_Active_Personnel }
		divide_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = 5000 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math_Display = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Scope = AAO }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Id = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Scope = AAJ }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Id = 2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Scope = AAG }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Id = 3 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Scope = AAA }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Id = 4 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Scope = AAC }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Id = 5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_Decision_GUI_Tab_Scope = AAB }
			}

		set_variable = { Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active = 0 }
		
		# Antarctica Task Force Alert

		add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes
	}

Antarctica_Tick = {

	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Week_Counter = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Month_Counter = 1 }
	
	for_each_loop = { # decrease mission timer
		array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array
		value = v
		index = i
		
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array^i > 0 } }
			
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Id_Array^i = 1 } } # Mission 1
				add_to_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array^i = -3.33 } # 30 days, each day is 3.33%
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array^i = 0 }

	# Daily Checks for supply and mechanics
	# Done like this (no every_country) for better performance
	AAA = {
		# Supply Calculations
		set_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = Antarctica_Active_Personnel }
		divide_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = 5000 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math_Display = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
		subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
	}
	AAC = {

		divide_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = 5000 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math_Display = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
		subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
	}
	AAG = {
		# Weapons Testing Mechanic Checks
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Testing_Enabled }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Timers
				value = v
				index = i
				
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Timers^i = -1 }
			}
			
			if = { # Ho 229 is timed out
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Timers^0 = 0 }
					is_in_array = {
						array = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array
						value = 1
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_1_Completed }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^0 > 66 }
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.200
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^0 > 33 }
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.201
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^0 > 0 }
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^0 = 0 }
						}
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.202
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Ho 229 is at 100%
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^0 = 100 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^0 > 100 }
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array
						value = 1
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_1_Completed }
				}
				country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.203
			}
			
			if = { # Me P1110 is at 100%
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^1 = 100 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^1 > 100 }
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array
						value = 2
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_2_Completed }
				}
				country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.210
			}
			
			if = { # Bo 115 is timed out
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Timers^2 = 0 }
					is_in_array = {
						array = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array
						value = 3
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_3_Completed }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^2 > 66 }
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.220
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^2 > 33 }
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.221
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^2 > 0 }
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^2 = 0 }
						}
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.222
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Bo 115 is at 100%
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^2 = 100 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^2 > 100 }
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array
						value = 3
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_3_Completed }
				}
				country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.223
			}
			
			if = { # Ho 18 is at 100%
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^3 = 100 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array_Success^3 > 100 }
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_Array
						value = 4
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Research_4_Completed }
				}
				country_event = antarctica_aag_testing.230
			}
		}
		# Weapons Testing Mechanic Tile Check
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { Antarctic_Special_Missions_1_AAG_Tile_Switch > 0 } }
			add_to_variable = { Antarctic_Special_Missions_1_AAG_Tile_Switch = -1 }
		}
		
		# For standard supply calculations
		if = { # 
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_Equipment_Change_Locked } }
			
			set_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = Antarctica_Active_Personnel }
			divide_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = 5000 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math_Display = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
			subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
		}
		else = { # For NS Survival calculations and population decrease
			if = { # Checking this, just in case
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = 0 } }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = Antarctica_AAG_Survival_Supply_Usage }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = Antarctica_Equipment
					min = 0
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_AAG_Survival_Supply_Usage < Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Survival_Mech_Max_Use }
						NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = 0 } }
						NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel < 22 } } # Random value from effects line 761
					}
				}
				Antarctica_AAG_Survival_Decrease_Personnel = yes
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { Antarctica_AAG_Survival_Days_Under_Max_Supply = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	AAJ = {

	AAO = {
		# Supply Calculations
		set_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = Antarctica_Active_Personnel }
		divide_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = 5000 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math_Display = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
		subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Mechanic_Enabled
			}
			# PERT Timer
			calculate_PERT_decrease_timers = yes
			
			# PERT Errors
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Time_Since_Last_Action = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Time_Since_Last_Action > 30 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Electronics_Error_Occurred }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Airframe_Error_Occurred }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_REV_Error_Occurred }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Testing_Error_Occurred }
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { # Electronics Error
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Activity_Frames^17 = 2 }
						}
						set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Electronics_Error_Occurred
					}
					1 = { # Airframe Error
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Activity_Frames^36 = 2 }
						}
						set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Airframe_Error_Occurred
					}
					1 = { # Guidance Error
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Activity_Frames^52 = 2 }
						}
						set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_REV_Error_Occurred
					}
					1 = { # Testing Error
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Activity_Frames^36 = 1 }
						}
						set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Testing_Error_Occurred
					}
				}
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Time_Since_Last_Action = 0 }
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Electronics_Error_Occurred
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Error_Occurred_Days = 0.5 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Airframe_Error_Occurred
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Error_Occurred_Days = 0.5 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_REV_Error_Occurred
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Error_Occurred_Days = 0.5 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Testing_Error_Occurred
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Error_Occurred_Days = 0.5 }
			}
			
			# Run Progress Report automatically if it's been over 3 months
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Time_Since_Last_Action > 90 }
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Electronics_Error_Occurred
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Airframe_Error_Occurred
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_REV_Error_Occurred
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Testing_Error_Occurred
					}
				}
				calculate_PERT_time_to_get_to_each_event = yes
				add_political_power = -5
				
				if = { # redundant
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Electronics_Error_Occurred
							has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Airframe_Error_Occurred
							has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_REV_Error_Occurred
							has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Testing_Error_Occurred
						}
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aao_pert.1000
				}
				else = {
					country_event = antarctica_aao_pert.1001
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_PERT_Decision_Array_Integrated_Timer^0 = 14 }
			}
		}
	}
	AAR = {
		# Supply Calculations
		set_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = Antarctica_Active_Personnel }
		divide_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = 5000 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math_Display = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
		subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
	}
	AAI = {
		# Supply Calculations
		set_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = Antarctica_Active_Personnel }
		divide_temp_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math = 5000 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math_Display = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
		subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Math }
	}
	
	if = { # weekly decay for stats and mission supply, and AI mission selector
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Week_Counter = 7 }
		}
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Week_Counter = 0 }
		
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_Antarctic_nation = yes }
			
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization = -1 }
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = -1 }
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment_Decrease = 0 }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Scope_Array
				value = v
				index = i
				
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^i = THIS } }
					add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment_Decrease = -1 }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = Antarctica_Equipment_Decrease }
			
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					start_Antarctica_GUI_Mission_AI = yes
					
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							check_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment < 25 }
							check_variable = { Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active = Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Cap }
							is_ai = no
						}
					}
				}
				1 = {
					# Nothing
				}
			}
		}

		AAG = { # Supply crisis weekly personnel decay because no food and no medicine is bad
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAG_Survival_Mech_Enabled
				}
			}

			randomize_variable = {
				var = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Random_Decay
				distribution = uniform
				min = 1
				max = 6
			}
			round_variable = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Random_Decay
			subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_Active_Personnel = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Random_Decay }
			round_variable = Antarctica_Active_Personnel
			
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_AAG_Survival_Total_Loss = Antarctica_Active_Personnel_Random_Decay }
			
			Antarctica_AAG_Survival_Check_Game_Over = yes
			
			Antarctica_AAG_Survival_Check_Supply_Usage = yes
		}
		
		AAO = { # Additional cohesion handling for the OAA
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAO_Cohesion = -2 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = Antarctica_GUI_AAO_Cohesion
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = AAO_Cohesion_1
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = -2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = AAO_Cohesion_2
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = -1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = AAO_Cohesion_3
				}
				# Nothing
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = AAO_Cohesion_4
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = AAO_Cohesion_5
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Month_Counter = 30 }
		}
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Month_Counter = 0 }
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_Antarctic_nation = yes
			}
			
			# Monthly Capital Strike checks
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAA_Value > 74 }
					always = no # disabled for now
				}
				setup_Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_AAA = yes
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_Target = 1 }
				country_event = antarctica_alert_event.10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAB_Value > 74 }
					always = no # disabled for now
				}
				setup_Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_AAB = yes
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_Target = 2 }
				country_event = antarctica_alert_event.11
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAC_Value > 74 }
					always = no # disabled for now
				}
				setup_Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_AAC = yes
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_Target = 3 }
				country_event = antarctica_alert_event.12
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAG_Value > 74 }
					always = no # disabled for now
				}
				setup_Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_AAG = yes
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_Target = 4 }
				country_event = antarctica_alert_event.13
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAJ_Value > 74 }
					always = no # disabled for now
				}
				setup_Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_AAJ = yes
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_Target = 5 }
				country_event = antarctica_alert_event.14
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAO_Value > 74 }
					always = no # disabled for now
				}
				setup_Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_AAO = yes
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Capital_Special_Mission_Target = 6 }
				country_event = antarctica_alert_event.15
			}
			
			# Emergency check for task force errors
			set_variable = { Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active_Check = 0 }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Scope_Array
				value = v
				index = i
				
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^i = THIS } }
					add_to_variable = { Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active_Check = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctic_Special_Missions_Currently_Intercepting_Mission
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active_Check = 1 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active = Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active_Check }
			set_variable = { Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active_Check = 0 }
			
			# Antarctica Task Force Alert
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active < Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Cap }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { alert_id = 9000 }
				add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Extra Clamp, just in case
	clamp_all_Antarctica_variables = yes
	
	# Check for Zero Stats
	check_Antarctica_Variables_for_Zero = yes
}

check_Antarctica_Variables_for_Zero = { # YOU LOSE
	AAA = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization = 0 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_Militarization_Game_Over }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				randomize_variable = { var = Antarctica_Militarization distribution = uniform min = 25 max = 75 }
				round_variable = Antarctica_Militarization
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_Situation_Overview_Emergency_Militarization_mission_triggered
				}
				country_event = antarctica_aaa_alert_event.11
				set_country_flag = Antarctica_Militarization_Game_Over
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = Antarctica_Situation_Overview_Emergency_Militarization_mission_triggered
				country_event = antarctica_aaa_alert_event.10
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization < 25 }
			}
			# Antarctica Low Stat Alert
			set_temp_variable = { alert_id = 9001 }
			add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Stats_Alert_Clear = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = 0 }

run_Antarctica_GUI_Mission_1_Effect = {
	log_Antarctica_GUI_mission = yes
	var:global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = {
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization = -4 }
		add_political_power = 40
		
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index } }
			# Targeted Self - Demilitarize Nearby Area - 1
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 1 }
			fire_Antarctica_GUI_event = yes
		}
		else = {
			# Targeted Other - Conduct Jet Flyovers - 1.5
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 0.5 }
			fire_Antarctica_GUI_event = yes
			
			var:global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = {
				add_political_power = -20
			}
		}
		
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Id_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }
		
		clamp_all_Antarctica_variables = yes
		remove_one_Antarctic_Intelligence_Agent_Used = yes
	}
}

run_Antarctica_GUI_Mission_2_Effect = {
	log_Antarctica_GUI_mission = yes
	var:global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = {
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization = -4 }
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = 8 }
		
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index } }
			# Targeted Self - Run Border Patrols - 2
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 2 }
			fire_Antarctica_GUI_event = yes
		}
		else = {
			# Targeted Other - Conduct Scout Helicopter Flyovers - 2.5
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 0.5 }
			fire_Antarctica_GUI_event = yes
			
			var:global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = {
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = -4 }
			}
		}
		
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }

	var:global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = {
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization = -9 }
		
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index } }
			# Targeted self
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAO } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAA_Value = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAC_Value = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAG_Value = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAJ_Value = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAB } }

		else = { # Targeted other

run_Antarctica_GUI_Mission_29_Effect = {
	log_Antarctica_GUI_mission = yes
	var:global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = {
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = -4 }
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = 8 }
		
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index } }
			# Targeted Self - Update Seafloor Maps - 29
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 29 }
			fire_Antarctica_GUI_event = yes
		}
		else = {
			# Targeted Other - Update Seafloor Maps - 29.5
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 29 }
			#add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 0.5 }
			fire_Antarctica_GUI_event = yes
			
			var:global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = {
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = -4 }
			}
		}
		
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }

				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAJ } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAA_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAC_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAG_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAO_Value = -1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAC } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAA_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAO_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAG_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAJ_Value = -1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAA } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAO_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAC_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAG_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAJ_Value = -1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAR } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAA_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAO_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAG_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAJ_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAC_Value = -1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAI } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAA_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAO_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAG_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAJ_Value = -1 }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAC_Value = -1 }
			}
			
			# Targeted Self - Confiscate Foreign Buoys - 32
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 32 }
			fire_Antarctica_GUI_event = yes
		}
		else = { # Targeted other
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAO } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAO_Value = -2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAB } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAB_Value = -2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAG } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAG_Value = -2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAJ } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAJ_Value = -2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAC } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAC_Value = -2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAA } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAA_Value = -2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAR } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAR_Value = -2 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = AAI } }
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Intel_on_AAI_Value = -2 }
			}
			
			# Targeted Other - Confiscate Foreign Buoys - 32.5
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 32 }
			#add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 0.5 }
			fire_Antarctica_GUI_event = yes
			
			var:global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = {
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = -3 }
			}
		}
		
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }
		set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Id_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index = 0 }
		
		clamp_all_Antarctica_variables = yes
		remove_one_Antarctic_Intelligence_Agent_Used = yes
	}
}

log_Antarctica_GUI_mission = {
	# global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Tile	 				# holds the list of tile locations of all completed missions
	# global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Dates 				# holds the list of dates of all completed missions
	# global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Source	 			# holds the list of source tags of all completed missions
	# global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Target	 			# holds the list of target tags of all completed missions
	# global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_IDs	 				# holds the list of IDs of all completed missions
	
	set_variable = { temp = global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index }
	add_to_variable = { temp = 1 }
	add_to_array = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Tile = temp }
	add_to_array = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Dates = global.date } # Starts to 60987.120, increases by 0.01 every hour
	add_to_array = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Source = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index }
	add_to_array = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_Target = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index }
	add_to_array = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Log_Completion_IDs = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Id_Array^global.Antarctica_GUI_Mission_Effect_Index }
}

			#days = var:Antarctica_GUI_event_days
		}
	}
	
	set_variable = { broken_event_finder = 0 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_variable = 0 }
	#set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_event_days = 0 }
}

start_Antarctica_GUI_Mission_AI = {

	# Pick a tile
	randomize_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_Mission_AI_Tile
		distribution = uniform
		min = 1
		max = 1024
	}
	round_variable = Antarctica_GUI_Mission_AI_Tile
	
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Selected_State = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Numbers_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Mission_AI_Tile }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Selected_Scope = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Scope_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Mission_AI_Tile }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Index = Antarctica_GUI_Mission_AI_Tile }
	
	# Check if tile is empty
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = 0 }
		}
		
		# Check if the tile is controlled by us
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_Selected_Scope = THIS }
			}
			# Tile is controlled by us. Check what type of tile it is, then pick a mission from the possible ones
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_AGS_Inland_Tile = yes
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { 
						# Mission 1
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = 100 } # 30 days
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = THIS } # The AI's scope
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = Antarctica_GUI_Selected_Scope } # 
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Id_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = 1 } # Mission 1 happening in this tile
						
						log = "Started by [THIS.GetFlag] in [?Antarctica_GUI_Selected_Scope.GetFlag], Mission 1"
						
						add_one_Antarctic_Intelligence_Agent_Used = yes
						
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							OR = {
								check_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization < 25 }
								has_political_power > 200 
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 3
							OR = {
								check_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization > 75 }
								has_political_power < 25
							}
						}
					}
					1 = {
						# Mission 2
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = 100 } # 28 days
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = THIS } # The AI's scope
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = Antarctica_GUI_Selected_Scope } # 
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Id_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = 2 } # Mission 2 happening in this tile
						
						log = "Started by [THIS.GetFlag] in [?Antarctica_GUI_Selected_Scope.GetFlag], Mission 2"
						
						add_one_Antarctic_Intelligence_Agent_Used = yes
						
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							OR = {
								check_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization < 25 }
								check_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy > 75 }
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 3
							OR = {
								check_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization > 75 }
								check_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy < 25 }
							}
						}
					}
					1 = {
						# Mission 4
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Progress_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = 100 } # 30 days
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Source_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = THIS } # The AI's scope
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Scope_Target_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = Antarctica_GUI_Selected_Scope } # The current tile scope
						set_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Mission_Id_Array^Antarctica_GUI_Index = 4 } # Mission 4 happening in this tile
						
						log = "Started by [THIS.GetFlag] in [?Antarctica_GUI_Selected_Scope.GetFlag], Mission 4"
						
						add_one_Antarctic_Intelligence_Agent_Used = yes
						
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							OR = {

	random_list = {
		1 = {
			set_country_flag = setting_Additional_Antarctica_GUI_Mission
			start_Antarctica_GUI_Mission_AI = yes
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = setting_Additional_Antarctica_GUI_Mission
					check_variable = { Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Active = Antarctic_Intelligence_Agents_Cap }
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
		}

		}
